function parseJokes(text) { const blocks = text.trim().split(/\n\s*\n/); const jokes = []; for (const block of blocks) { const lines = block.trim().split(”\n”).map(l => l.trim()).filter(Boolean); if (lines.length < 2) continue; const description = lines[lines.length - 1]; const jokeText = lines.slice(0, -1).join(” “); jokes.push({ jokeText, description }); } return jokes; } async function loadFont() { const binary = atob(FONT_B64); const bytes = new Uint8Array(binary.length); for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) bytes[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i); const font = new FontFace(“CalSans”, bytes.buffer, { weight: “700” }); await font.load(); document.fonts.add(font); } async function generateImage(jokeText) { const W = 2000, H = 3000; const canvas = document.createElement(“canvas”); canvas.width = W; canvas.height = H; const ctx = canvas.getContext(“2d”); ctx.fillStyle = “#ffffff”; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H); const paddingX = 130; const maxWidth = W - paddingX * 2; function wrapText(text, fontSize) { ctx.font = `bold ${fontSize}px CalSans`; const words = text.split(” “); const lines = []; let line = “”; for (const word of words) { const test = line ? line + “ “ + word : word; if (ctx.measureText(test).width > maxWidth && line) { lines.push(line); line = word; } else { line = test; } } if (line) lines.push(line); return lines; } let fontSize = 150; let lines = []; while (fontSize >= 60) { lines = wrapText(jokeText, fontSize); const totalH = lines.length * fontSize * 1.25; if (totalH <= H - 500) break; fontSize -= 4; } const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.25; const totalTextH = lines.length * lineHeight; const startY = (H - totalTextH) / 2 + fontSize * 0.82; ctx.fillStyle = “#000000”; ctx.font = `bold ${fontSize}px CalSans`; ctx.textAlign = “center”; ctx.textBaseline = “alphabetic”; lines.forEach((line, i) => { ctx.fillText(line, W / 2, startY + i * lineHeight); }); return canvas.toDataURL(“image/png”); } export default function App() { const [input, setInput] = useState(””); const [jokes, setJokes] = useState([]); const [images, setImages] = useState([]); const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false); const textareaRef = useRef(null); const fontLoadedRef = useRef(false); const ensureFont = useCallback(async () => { if (fontLoadedRef.current) return; await loadFont(); fontLoadedRef.current = true; }, []); const handlePaste = useCallback(async () => { try { const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText(); setInput(text); } catch { textareaRef.current?.focus(); } }, []); const handleExtract = useCallback(async () => { if (!input.trim()) return; setLoading(true); try { await ensureFont(); const parsed = parseJokes(input); setJokes(parsed); const imgs = []; for (const j of parsed) { imgs.push(await generateImage(j.jokeText)); } setImages(imgs); } finally { setLoading(false); } }, [input, ensureFont]); const btnYellow = { background: “rgba(255,200,80,0.07)”, border: “1px solid
